let max : <extra_id_0> = fix (case self => (
    case (~zero @, n) => n
    case (n, ~zero @) => n
    case (~succ m, ~succ n) => ~succ (self(m, n))
)) in
let depth : <extra_id_1> = fix (case self => (
    case (~leaf @) => ~zero @
    case (~node (l, r)) => ~succ ((max)((self)(l), (self)(r)))
)) in

    case (~zero @, n) => n 
    case (~succ m, n) => ~succ (self(m, n))

let add : <extra_id_0> = fix (case self => ( 
    case (~zero @, n) => n 
    case (~succ m, n) => ~succ (self(m, n))
)) in
let isOdd : <extra_id_1> = fix (case self => ( 
    case (~zero @) => ~false @
    case (~succ ~zero @) => ~true @
    case (~succ ~succ n) => self(n)
)) in
let sumOddUpTo : <extra_id_2> = fix (case self => ( 
    case (~zero @) => ~zero @
    case n => if (isOdd)(n) then
                (add)(n, (self)((~pred n)))
              else
                (self)((~pred n))
)) in

    case (~zero @, n) => n 
    case (~succ m, n) => ~succ (self(m, n))
)) in

    case (~zero @) => ~false @
    case (~succ ~zero @) => ~true @
    case (~succ ~succ n) => self(n)

)) in

let max : <extra_id_0> = fix (case self => (
    case (~zero @, n) => n
    case (n, ~zero @) => n
    case (~succ m, ~succ n) => ~succ (self(m, n))
)) in
let depth : <extra_id_1> = fix (case self => (
    case (~leaf @) => ~zero @
    case (~node (l, r)) => ~succ ((max)((self)(l), (self)(r)))
)) in

let max : <extra_id_0> = fix (case self => (
    case (~zero @, n) => n
    case (n, ~zero @) => n
    case (~succ m, ~succ n) => ~succ (self(m, n))
)) in
let depth : <extra_id_1> = fix (case self => (
    case (~leaf @) => ~zero @
    case (~node (l, r)) => ~succ ((max)((self)(l), (self)(r)))
)) in

let max : <extra_id_0> = fix (case self => (
    case (~zero @, n) => n
    case (n, ~zero @) => n
    case (~succ m, ~succ n) => ~succ (self(m, n))
)) in
let depth : <extra_id_1> = fix (case self => (
    case (~leaf @) => ~zero @
    case (~node (l, r)) => ~succ ((max)((self)(l), (self)(r)))
)) in
